#include<cmath>#include<cassert>#include<exception>#include<iostream>#include<stdexcept>//------}-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------//Name:Addition//Input:a-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Input:b-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Computation:Computea+b//Exception:Throwanstd::invalid_argumentexceptionifeitheraorbare3//Exception:Throwanstd::out_of_rangeexceptioniftheresultislessthan-16//Exception:Throwanstd::out_of_rangeexceptioniftheresultisgreaterthan24//Returns:a+bifnoexceptionisthrown//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------template<typenameT>TAddition(Ta,Tb){//------------------------------------------------------------------------//DONOTMODIFYTHISFUNCTIONWHILEYOUWORKONDEVELOPINGYOURTESTCASES//------------------------------------------------------------------------if(a==3)throwstd::invalid_argument("");if(b==3)throwstd::invalid_argument("");Tvalue=a+b;if(value<-16)throwstd::out_of_range("");if(value>24)throwstd::out_of_range("");returnvalue;}//--------------------------------------------------------------------//NOWIT'STIMETOTESTOUTTHEAddition(a,b)FUNCTION//ADDTESTCASESTHATHANDLEALLPOSSIBLECODEPATHSATLEASTONETIME//USEATLEASTTHREEDIFFERENTTEMPLATEDTYPESFORYOURTTYPE,MEANING//USEint,float,double,short,charTOTESTOUTDIFFERENTTYPES//-------------------------------------------------------------------intmain(){//TESTCASE1try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE1-";intresult=Addition<int>(0,0);if(result==0)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition(0,0)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition(0,0)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE2-a==3throwsinvalid_argumenttry{std::cout<<"TESTCASE2-";floatresult=Addition<float>(3.0f,5.0f);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition(3.0f,5.0f)SHOULDTHROWinvalid_argument"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-WRONGEXCEPTIONTYPETHROWN"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE3-b==3throwsinvalid_argumenttry{std::cout<<"TESTCASE3-";doubleresult=Addition<double>(5.5,3.0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition(5.5,3.0)SHOULDTHROWinvalid_argument"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-WRONGEXCEPTIONTYPETHROWN"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE4-result<-16throwsout_of_rangetry{std::cout<<"TESTCASE4-";shortresult=Addition<short>(-10,-8);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition(-10,-8)SHOULDTHROWout_of_range"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-WRONGEXCEPTIONTYPETHROWN"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE5-result>24throwsout_of_rangetry{std::cout<<"TESTCASE5-";doubleresult=Addition<double>(20.5,4.0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition(20.5,4.0)SHOULDTHROWout_of_range"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-WRONGEXCEPTIONTYPETHROWN"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE6-anothersuccessfulcasewithdifferenttypetry{std::cout<<"TESTCASE6-";floatresult=Addition<float>(10.5f,2.5f);if(result==13.0f)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition(10.5f,2.5f)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition(10.5f,2.5f)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}return0;}

/**SignalDecoder-CosmicMessageAssignment*Decodesbinarytransmissionsfollowingamulti-stepprocess:*1.Readeachlinefromfileintoavectorofstrings*2.Convertbinary(groupsof8)toASCIIcharacters*3.Extractevery3rdcharacterstartingatindex1*4.Keeponlyalphanumericcharacters*5.Reverseeachstring,thencombineforthefullmessage*/#include<iostream>#include<fstream>#include<vector>#include<string>#include<algorithm>#include<cctype>voidprintVector(conststd::vector<std::string>&vec){for(conststd::string&s:vec){std::cout<<s<<"\n";}std::cout<<"\n";}intmain(){std::vector<std::string>lines;std::ifstreaminFile("signal.txt");if(!inFile){std::cerr<<"Error:Couldnotopensignal.txt\n";return1;}std::stringline;while(std::getline(inFile,line)){if(!line.empty()){lines.push_back(line);}}inFile.close();std::cout<<"Linesreadfromfile:"<<lines.size()<<"\n\n";for(std::string&s:lines){std::stringascii="";for(size_ti=0;i+8<=s.size();i+=8){std::stringbyte=s.substr(i,8);intvalue=std::stoi(byte,nullptr,2);ascii+=static_cast<char>(value);}s=ascii;}std::cout<<"===Step2:Binary→ASCII===\n";printVector(lines);for(std::string&s:lines){std::stringextracted="";for(size_ti=1;i<s.size();i+=3){extracted+=s[i];}s=extracted;}std::cout<<"===Step3:Every3rdCharacter(startingatindex1)===\n";printVector(lines);for(std::string&s:lines){std::stringfiltered="";for(charc:s){if(isalnum(c)){filtered+=c;}}s=filtered;}std::cout<<"===Step4):Letters&NumbersOnly===\n";printVector(lines);for(std::string&s:lines){std::reverse(s.begin(),s.end());}std::cout<<"===Step5:ReversedStrings===\n";printVector(lines);std::stringfullMessage="";for(conststd::string&s:lines){fullMessage+=s;}std::cout<<"===FULLCOSMICMESSAGE===\n";std::cout<<fullMessage<<"\n";return0;}
#include<iostream>#include<string>#include<stdexcept>shortConvertToShort(conststd::string&str){conststd::stringerrorMessage="ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger!";//Emptystringisinvalidif(str.empty()){throwstd::invalid_argument(errorMessage);}inti=0;intsign=1;if(str[0]=='+'){i=1;}elseif(str[0]=='-'){sign=-1;i=1;}//Checkifthestringhascharactersafterthesignif(i>=(int)str.size()){throwstd::invalid_argument(errorMessage);}//Parsedigitsbeforethedecimalpointintresult=0;boolhasDigits=false;while(i<(int)str.size()&&str[i]!='.'){if(str[i]<'0'||str[i]>'9'){throwstd::invalid_argument(errorMessage);}result=result*10+(str[i]-'0');if(result>32768){throwstd::invalid_argument(errorMessage);}hasDigits=true;i++;}if(!hasDigits){throwstd::invalid_argument(errorMessage);}//Decimalpointif(i<(int)str.size()&&str[i]=='.'){i++;while(i<(int)str.size()){if(str[i]!='0'){throwstd::invalid_argument(errorMessage);}i++;}}intsignedResult=sign*result;if(signedResult<-32768||signedResult>32767){throwstd::invalid_argument(errorMessage);}returnstatic_cast<short>(signedResult);}intmain(){std::stringinput;std::stringresponse;do{std::cout<<"Enteravaluetoconvert:";std::cin>>input;try{shortvalue=ConvertToShort(input);std::cout<<"Convertedvalue:"<<value<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&e){std::cout<<e.what()<<std::endl;}while(true){std::cout<<"Convertanothervalue?(y/n):";std::cin>>response;if(response=]="y"||response=="Y"){break;}elseif(response=="n"||response=="N"){return0;}else{std::cout<<"Invalidresponse.Pleaseenter'y'or'n'."<<std::endl;}}}while(response=="y"||response=="Y");return0;}

#include<algorithm>#include<cctype>#include<fstream>#include<iostream>#include<string>#include<vector>voidPrintVector(conststd::vector<std::string>&lines){for(conststd::string&line:lines){std::cout<<line<<std::endl;}std::cout<<std::endl;}charBinaryToChar(conststd::string&bits){intvalue=0;for(charbit:bits){value*=2;if(bit=='1'){value+=1;}}returnstatic_cast)<char>(value);}intmain(){std::ifstreamfin("signal.txt");if(!fin){std::cout<<"Couldnotopensignal.txt"<<std::endl;return1;}std::vector<std::string>lines;std::stringline;while(std::getline(fin,line)){lines.push_back(line);}//Step2:ConverteachlinefrombinarybytestoASCIIstd::vector<std::string>decoded(lines.size());for(std::size_ti=0;i<lines.size();i++){for(std::size_tj=0;j+7<lines[i].size();j+=8){decoded[i]+=BinaryToChar(lines[i].substr(j,8));}}PrintVector(decoded);//Step3:Keepthesecondcharacter,theneverythirdafterthatfor(std::string&current:decoded){std::stringreduced;for(std::size_ti=1;i<current.size();i+=3){reduced+=current[i];}current=reduced;}PrintVector(decoded);//Step4:Keeponlylettersandnumbersfor(std::string&current:decoded){std::stringfiltered;for(charch:current){if(std::isalnum(static_cast<unsignedchar>(ch))){filtered+=ch;}}current=filtered;}PrintVector(decoded);//Step5:Reverseeachlinefor(std::string&current:decoded){std::reverse(current.begin(),current.end());}PrintVector(decoded);//Combinefinalmessagestd::stringfinalMessage;for(conststd::string&current:decoded){finalMessage+=current;}std::cout<<finalMessage<<std::endl;return0;}
#include<cmath>#include<cassert>#include<exception>#include<iostream>//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------//Name:Subtraction//Input:a-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Input:b-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Computation:Computea-b//Exception:Throwanstd::invalid_argumentexceptionifa<0//Exception:Throwanstd::invalid_argumentexceptionifb>0//Exception:Throwanstd::out_of_rangeexceptioniftheresultislessthan2//Exception:Throwanstd::out_of_rangeexceptioniftheresultisgreaterthan18//Returns:a-bifnoexceptionisthrown//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------template<typenameT>TSubtraction(Ta,Tb){//------------------------------------------------------------------------//DONOTMODIFYTHISFUNCTIONWHILEYOUWORKONDEVELOPINGYOURTESTCASES//------------------------------------------------------------------------if(a<0)throwstd::invalid_argument("");if(b>0)throwstd::invalid_argument("");Tvalue=a-b;if(value<2)throwstd::out_of_range("");if(value>18)throwstd::out_of_range("");returnvalue;}intmain(){//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE1-Happypath:validintinputs,resultinrange[2,18]//a>=0,b<=0,result=3-0=3(inrange)//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE1-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(3,0);if(result==3)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(3,0)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(3,0)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE2-invalid_argument:a<0(int)//Expectsstd::invalid_argumenttobethrown//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE2-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(-1,0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(-1,0)SHOULDHAVETHROWNinvalid_argument"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(-1,0)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE3-invalid_argument:b>0(int)//Expectsstd::invalid_argumenttobethrown//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE3-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(5,3);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(5,3)SHOULDHAVETHROWNinvalid_argument"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(5,3)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE4-out_of_range:result<2(int)//a=2,b=0=>result=2-0=2,whichisNOT<2,sousea=1,b=0=>1<2//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE4-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(1,0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(1,0)SHOULDHAVETHROWNout_of_range"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(1,0)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE5-out_of_range:result>18(int)//a=20,b=0=>result=20>18//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE5-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(20,0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(20,0)SHOULDHAVETHROWNout_of_range"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(20,0)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE6-Happypath:boundaryresultexactly2(int)//a=2,b=0=>result=2,whichistheminimumallowedvalue//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE6-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(2,0);if(result==2)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(2,0)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(2,0)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE7-Happypath:boundaryresultexactly18(int)//a=18,b=0=>result=18,whichisthemaximumallowedvalue//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE7-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(18,0);if(result==18)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(18,0)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(18,0)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE8-Happypath:floattype,bisnegative//a=10.0f,b=-5.0f=>result=15.0f(inrange)//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE8-";floatresult=Subtraction<float>(10.0f,-5.0f);if(result==15.0f)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<float>(10.0f,-5.0f)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<float>(10.0f,-5.0f)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE9-invalid_argument:a<0,floattype//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE9-";floatresult=Subtraction<float>(-1.0f,-5.0f);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<float>(-1.0f,-5.0f)SHOULDHAVETHROWNinvalid_argument"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<float>(-1.0f,-5.0f)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE10-out_of_range:result>18,floattype//a=20.0f,b=-5.0f=>result=25.0f>18//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE10-";floatresult=Subtraction<float>(20.0f,-5.0f);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<float>(20.0f,-5.0f)SHOULDHAVETHROWNout_of_range"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<float>(20.0f,-5.0f)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//--------)-----------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE11-Happypath:doubletype//a=12.5,b=-3.5=>result=16.0(inrange)//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE11-";doubleresult=Subtraction<double>(12.5,-3.5);if(result==16.0)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<double>(12.5,-3.5)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<double>(12.5,-3.5)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE12-out_of_range:result<2,doubletype//a=1.0,b=0.0=>result=1.0<2//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE12-";doubleresult=Subtraction<double>(1.0,0.0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<double>(1.0,0.0)SHOULDHAVETHROWNout_of_range"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<double>(1.0,0.0)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE13-Happypath:shorttype//a=10,b=0=>result=10(inrange)//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE13-";shortresult=Subtraction<short>(10,0);if(result==10)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<short>(10,0)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<short>(10,0)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE14-invalid_argument:b>0,shorttype//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE14-";shortresult=Subtraction<short>(10,2);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<short>(10,2)SHOULDHAVETHROWNinvalid_argument"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<short>(10,2)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}return0;}
#include<iostream>#include<string>#include<stdexcept>usingnamespacestd;shortConvertToShort(conststd::string&input){if(input.empty())throwinvalid_argument("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");inti=0;boolnegative=false;if(input[i]=='+'||input[i]=='-'){negative=(input[i]=='-');i++;if(i>=input.length())throwinvalid_argument("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");}longlongvalue=0;boolhasDigit=false;boolhasDecimal=false;for(;i<input.length();i++){charch=input[i];if(ch>='0'&&ch<='9'){hasDigit=true;intdigit=ch-'0';if(!hasDecimal){v)alue=value*10+digit;if((!negative&&value>32767)||(negative&&value>32768))throwinvalid_argument("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");}else{if(digit!=0)throwinvalid_argument("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");}}elseif(ch=='.'){if(hasDecimal||!hasDigit)throwinvalid_argument("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");hasDecimal=true;}else{throwinvalid_argument("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");}}if(!hasDigit)throwinvalid_argument("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");if(negative)value=-value;if(value<-32768||value>32767)throwinvalid_argument("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");return(short)value;}intmain(){stringinput;charagain;do{cout<<"Enterastring:";cin>>input;try{shortresult=ConvertToShort(input);cout<<"Convertedvalue:"<<result<<endl;}catch(constinvalid_argument&e){cout<<e.what()<<endl;}while(true){cout<<"Convertanothervalue?(Y/N):";cin>>again;if(again=='Y'||again=='y'||again=='N'||again=='n')break;cout<<"Invalidresponse.PleaseenterYorN."<<endl;}}while(again=='Y'||again=='y');return0;}

#include<cmath>#include<cassert>#include<exception>#include<iostream>//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------//Name:Subtraction//Input:a-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Input:b-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Computation:Computea-b//Exception:Throwanstd::invalid_argumentexceptionifa<0//Exception:Throwanstd::invalid_argumentexceptionifb>0//Exception:Throwanstd::out_of_rangeexceptioniftheresultislessthan2//Exception:Throwanstd::out_of_rangeexceptioniftheresultisgreaterthan18//Returns:a-bifnoexceptionisthrown//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------template<typenameT>TSubtraction(Ta,Tb){//------------------------------------------------------------------------//DONOTMODIFYTHISFUNCTIONWHILEYOUWORKONDEVELOPINGYOURTESTCASES//------------------------------------------------------------------------if(a<0)throwstd::invalid_argument("");if(b>0)throwstd::invalid_argument("");Tvalue=a-b;if(value<2)throwstd::out_of_range("");if(value>18)throwstd::out_of_range("");returnvalue;}//--------------------------------------------------------------------//NOWIT'STIMETOTESTOUTTHESubtraction(a,b)FUNCTION//ADDTESTCASESTHATHANDLEALLPOSSIBLECODEPATHSATLEASTONETIME//USEATLEASTTHREEDIFFERENTTEMPLATEDTYPESFORYOURTTYPE,MEANING//USEint,float,double,short,charTOTESTOUTDIFFERENTTYPES//-------------------------------------------------------------------intmain(){//TESTCASE1//correctsubtractiontry{std::cout<<"TESTCASE1-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(3,0);if(result==3)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(0,0)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(0,0)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE2//a<0,throwinvalid_argument,testfloattry{std::cout<<"TESTCASE2-";floatresult=Subtraction<float>(-3.0f,0.0f);std::cout<<"F)AILURE-Subtraction<float>(-3.0f,0.0f)SHOULDTHROWinvalid_argument"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd:: //CIS254203/29/2026HW8#include<iostream>#include<string>#include<stdexcept>conststd::stringERROR_MESSAGE="ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger";shortConvertToShort(conststd::string&input);//AhelpertokeepthemainlogiccleanboolIsDigit(charc){return(c>='0'&&c<='9');}shortConvertToShort(conststd::string&input){//Ifthestringisempty,exitearlyif(input.empty()){throwstd::invalid_argument(ERROR_MESSAGE);}intindex=0;intlength=static_cast<int>(input.length());boolisNegative=false;//First,seeifthere'sasignatthebeginningif(input[index]=='+'||input[index]=='-'){if(input[index]=='-'){isNegative=true;}index++;//Movepastthesigntogettothedigits}//Ifwehadasignbutnothingafterit,that'sanerrorif(index>=length){throwstd::invalid_argument(ERROR_MESSAGE);}longlongvalue=0;booldecimalPointFound=false;booldigitFound=false;//Nowloopthroughthestringcharacterbycharacterwhile(index<length){charcurrent=input[index];if(IsDigit(current)){digitFound=true;intdigit=current-'0';//Safetyfirst:Checkforoverflowbeforewemultiplyandaddthedigit//Thispreventsthenumberfrom"wrappingaround"andprovidingafalsereadingif(!isNegative){if(value>(32767-digit)/10){throwstd::invalid_argument(ERROR_MESSAGE);}}else{//Note:-32768hasaslightlylargermagnitudethan32767if(value>(32768LL-digit)/10){throwstd::invalid_argument(ERROR_MESSAGE);}}value=value)*10+digit;}elseif(current=='.'){//Weonlyallowasingledecimalpointif(decimalPointFound){throwstd::invalid_argument(ERROR_MESSAGE);}decimalPointFound=true;}else{//Ifit'snotadigitoradot,itshouldn'tbeherethrowstd::invalid_argument(ERROR_MESSAGE);}index++;}//Sincewe'reconvertingtoashort,weneedtomakesureanycharactersafteradecimalpointarejustzeros.if(decimalPointFound){intdotIndex=static_cast<int>(input.find('.'));for(inti=dotIndex+1;i<length;i++){if(input[i]!='0'){throwstd::invalid_argument(ERROR_MESSAGE);//Foundanon-zerodecimalvalue}}}//Makesureweactuallyfoundnumberstoworkwithif(!digitFound){throwstd::invalid_argument(ERROR_MESSAGE);}//TimetoapplythenegativesignifwefoundoneearlierlonglongfinalValue=value;if(isNegative){finalValue=-finalValue;}//Onefinalchecktomakesurethenumberfitsintothe16-bitsignedrangeif(finalValue<-32768||finalValue>32767){throwstd::invalid_argument(ERROR_MESSAGE);}returnstatic_cast<short>(finalValue);}intmain(){boolrunning=true;while(running){std::stringinput;std::cout<<"Enterastringtoconvert:"<<std::endl;std::getline(std::cin,input);try{//Attempttheconversionandshowtheresultifitworksshortresult=ConvertToShort(input);std::cout<<"Convertedvalue:"<<result<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&e){//IfanythingwentwronginConvertToShort,wecatchithereandshowtheerrorstd::cout<<e.what()<<std::endl;}//NowasktheuseriftheywanttogoagainboolvalidResponse=false;while(!validResponse){std::stringresponse;std::cout<<"Convertanothervalue?(Y/N):"<<std::endl;std::getline(std::cin,response);if(response=="Y"||response=="y"){validResponse=true;//Loopmainagain}elseif(response=="N"||response=="n"){validResponse=true;running=false;//Exittheprogram}else{//Iftheytypedsomethinginvalid,keepaskinguntiltheygiveusaYorNstd::cout<<"Invalidresponse.PleaseenterYorN."<<std::endl;}}}return0;}

#include<cmath>#include<exception>#include<iostream>#include<stdexcept>//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------//Developatemplatefunctionthathasthefollowingbehavior://Name:Modulus//Input:a-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Input:b-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Computation:Computetheremainderwhenaisdividedbyb//Exception:Throwanstd::invalid_argumentexceptionifb==0(sincedivisionbyzeroisnotallowed)//Exception:Throwanstd::out_of_rangeexceptioniftheresultofthemodulusoperationislessthan2//Returns:Theremainderwhenaisdividedbybifnoexceptionisthrown//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------template<typenameT>TModulus(Ta,Tb){if(b==0){throwstd::invalid_argument("Divisionbyzeroisnotallowed");}Tresult=static_cast<T>(std::fmod(a,b));if(result<2){throwstd::out_of_range("Resultislessthan2");}returnresult;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------//IFYOUMESSWITHTHISCODEBELOW,YOURFUNCTIONSTILLNEEDSTOWORK//WITHTHEFACTORYSETTINGSI'VESETUPFORALLLISTEDTESTCASES!!!!//-------------------------------------------------------------------intmain(){//TESTCASE1-(19/4)=4REMAINDER3SOTHEFUNCTIONRETURNS3try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE1-";inta=Modulus<int>(19,4);if(a==3)std::cout<<"PASSED"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-FUNCTIONDOESN'TRETURNTHEPROPERVALUE"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-NOEXCEPTIONSHOULDBETHROWNINTHISCASE"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE2-(19/6)=3REMAINDER1SOSHOULDTHROWSINCETHEREAMINDERISLESSTHAN2try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE2-";inta=Modulus<int>(19,6);std::cout<<"FAILURE-FUNCTIONSHOULDTHROWEX)CEPTION"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"PASSED"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE3-(19.5/2.0)=9.0REMAINDER1.5SOSHOULDTHROWSINCETHEREAMINDERISLESSTHAN2.0try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE3-";doublea=Modulus<double>(19.5,2.0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-FUNCTIONSHOULDTHROWEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"PASSED"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE4-(19.5f/8.0f)=2.0fREMAINDER3.5fSOTHEFUNCTIONRETURNS3.5ftry{std::cout<<"TESTCASE4-";floata=Modulus<float>(19.5f,8.0f);if(a==3.5f)std::cout<<"PASSED"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-FUNCTIONDOESN'TRETURNTHEPROPERVALUE"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-NOEXCEPTIONSHOULDBETHROWNINTHISCASE"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE5-(9.5/0.0)SHOULDTHROWSINCETHEDENOMINATORIS0.0try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE5-";doublea=Modulus<double>(9.5,0.0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-FUNCTIONSHOULDTHROWEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"PASSED"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE6-(7/0)SHOULDTHROWSINCETHEDENOMINATORIS0try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE6-";inta=Modulus<int>(7,0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-FUNCTIONSHOULDTHROWEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"PASSED"<<std::endl;}std::cout<<"DIDALLTESTCASESPASS?AREYOUFOLLOWINGBESTPRACTICES?SUBMITIFYOU'REREADY!"<<std::endl;return0;}

#include<iostream>#include<string>shortConvertToShort(conststd::string&input){//Stopfunctionandgiveerrormessageif(input.empty())throw"ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger";inti=0;//Assume+firstboolisNegative=false;if(input[i]=='+'||input[i]=='-'){//ChangetonegativeiftrueisNegative=(input[i]=='-');i++;if(i>=input.size())throw"ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger";}longresult=0;boolseenDigit=false;boolseenDecimal=false;//Loopthroughstringonecharacteratatimefor(;i<input.size();i++){charc=input[i];if(c=='.'){//invalidifseen2decimalsif(seenDecimal)throw"ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger";seenDecimal=true;//Checkafterdecimalifallzerosfor(intj=i+1;j<input.size();j++){if(input[j]!='0')throw"ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger";}break;}//Aftersign,onlyacceptednumbersarebetween0-9if(c<'0'||c>'9')throw"ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger";seenDigit=true;//Convertdigitcharactertointegerintdigit=c-'0';//Shiftpreviousnumbertheleftandaddcurrentnumberloopedresult=result*10+digit;//Goupto+32767if(!isNegative&&result>32767)throw"ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger";//Godownto-32768if(isNegative&&result>32768)throw"ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger";}//Nodigitsareinvalidif(!seenDigit)throw"ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger";//Makeoutputnegativeifnegativeif(isNegative)result=-result;//Changelongtoshortreturnstatic_cast<short>(result);}i}ntmain(){std::stringinput;std::stringchoice;do{std::cout<<"Enterastringtoconvert:";std::getline(std::cin,input);try{shortvalue=ConvertToShort(input);std::cout<<"Convertedvalue:"<<value<<std::endl;}//Catchthrownstringcatch(constchar*msg){std::cout<<msg<<std::endl;}while(true){std::cout<<"Convertanother?(Y/N):";std::getline(std::cin,choice);if(choice=="Y"||choice=="y"||choice=="N"||choice=="n")break;std::cout<<"Invalidinput.PleaseenterYorN."<<std::endl;}//Repeatifchoseny}while(choice=="Y"||choice=="y");return0;}

#include<cmath>#include<cassert>#include<exception>#include<iostream>//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------//Name:Subtraction//Input:a-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Input:b-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Computation:Computea-b//Exception:Throwanstd::invalid_argumentexceptionifa<0//Exception:Throwanstd::invalid_argumentexceptionifb>0//Exception:Throwanstd::out_of_rangeexceptioniftheresultislessthan2//Exception:Throwanstd::out_of_rangeexceptioniftheresultisgreaterthan18//Returns:a-bifnoexceptionisthrown//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------template<typenameT>TSubtraction(Ta,Tb){//------------------------------------------------------------------------//DONOTMODIFYTHISFUNCTIONWHILEYOUWORKONDEVELOPINGYOURTESTCASES//------------------------------------------------------------------------if(a<0)throwstd::invalid_argument("");if(b>0)throwstd::invalid_argument("");Tvalue=a-b;if(value<2)throwstd::out_of_range("");if(value>18)throwstd::out_of_range("");returnvalue;}intmain(){//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE1-Happypath:validintinputs,resultinrange[2,18]//a>=0,b<=0,result=3-0=3(inrange)//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE1-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(3,0);if(result==3)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(3,0)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(3,0)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//---------------------------)----------------------------------------------//TESTCASE2-invalid_argument:a<0(int)//Expectsstd::invalid_argumenttobethrown//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE2-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(-1,0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(-1,0)SHOULDHAVETHROWNinvalid_argument"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(-1,0)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE3-invalid_argument:b>0(int)//Expectsstd::invalid_argumenttobethrown//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE3-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(5,3);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(5,3)SHOULDHAVETHROWNinvalid_argument"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(5,3)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE4-out_of_range:result<2(int)//a=2,b=0=>result=2-0=2,whichisNOT<2,sousea=1,b=0=>1<2//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE4-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(1,0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(1,0)SHOULDHAVETHROWNout_of_range"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(1,0)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE5-out_of_range:result>18(int)//a=20,b=0=>result=20>18//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE5-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(20,0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(20,0)SHOULDHAVETHROWNout_of_range"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(20,0)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE6-Happypath:boundaryresultexactly2(int)//a=2,b=0=>result=2,whichistheminimumallowedvalue//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE6-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(2,0);if(result==2)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(2,0)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(2,0)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE7-Happypath:boundaryresultexactly18(int)//a=18,b=0=>result=18,whichisthemaximumallowedvalue//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE7-";intresult=Subtraction<int>(18,0);if(result==18)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(18,0)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction(18,0)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE8-Happypath:floattype,bisnegative//a=10.0f,b=-5.0f=>result=15.0f(inrange)//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE8-";floatresult=Subtraction<float>(10.0f,-5.0f);if(result==15.0f)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<float>(10.0f,-5.0f)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<float>(10.0f,-5.0f)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------//TESTCASE9-invalid_argument:a<0,floattype//-------------------------------------------------------------------------try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE9-";floatresult=Subtraction<float>(-1.0f,-5.0f);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<float>(-1.0f,-5.0f)SHOULDHAVETHROWNinvalid_argument"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Subtraction<float>(-1.0f,-5.0f)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//------------------------------------------------------------------- ////main.cpp//stringer////#include<iostream>#include<string>#include<stdexcept>shortConvertToShort(conststd::string&input){if(input.length()==0){throwstd::runtime_error("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");}intindex=0;boolisNegative=false;if(input[0]=='+'||input[0]=='-'){if(input.length()==1){throwstd::runtime_error("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");}if(input[0]=='-'){isNegative=true;}index=1;}longvalue=0;booldecimalFound=false;for(;index<input.length();index++){charc=input[index];if(c=='.'){if(decimalFound){throwstd::runtime_error("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");}decimalFound=true;for(intj=index+1;j<input.length();j++){if(input[j]!='0'){throwstd::runtime_error("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");}}break;}if(c<'0'||c>'9'){throwstd::runtime_error("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");}intdigit=c-'0';value=value*10)+digit;if(!isNegative&&value>32767){throwstd::runtime_error("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");}if(isNegative&&value>32768){throwstd::runtime_error("ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger");}}if(isNegative){value=-value;}returnstatic_cast<short>(value);}intmain(){std::stringinput;charchoice;do{std::cout<<"Enteravaluetoconvert:";std::cin>>input;try{shortresult=ConvertToShort(input);std::cout<<"Convertedvalue:"<<result<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&e){std::cout<<e.what()<<std::endl;}do{std::cout<<"Convertanothervalue?(Y/N):";std::cin>>choice;if(choice=='Y'||choice=='y'||choice=='N'||choice=='n'){break;}std::cout<<"Invalidinput.PleaseenterYorN."<<std::endl;}while(true);}while(choice=='Y'||choice=='y');return0;}
#include<cmath>#include<cassert>#include<exception>#include<iostream>#include<stdexcept>//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------//Name:Addition//Input:a-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Input:b-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Computation:Computea+b//Exception:Throwanstd::invalid_argumentexceptionifeitheraorbare3//Exception:Throwanstd::out_of_rangeexceptioniftheresultislessthan-16//Exception:Throwanstd::out_of_rangeexceptioniftheresultisgreaterthan24//Returns:a+bifnoexceptionisthrown//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------template<typenameT>TAddition(Ta,Tb){//------------------------------------------------------------------------//DONOTMODIFYTHISFUNCTIONWHILEYOUWORKONDEVELOPINGYOURTESTCASES//------------------------------------------------------------------------if(a==3)throwstd::invalid_argument("");if(b==3)throwstd::invalid_argument("");Tvalue=a+b;if(value<-16)throwstd::out_of_range("");if(value>24)throwstd::out_of_range("");returnvalue;}//--------------------------------------------------------------------//NOWIT'STIMETOTESTOUTTHEAddition(a,b)FUNCTION//ADDTESTCASESTHATHANDLEALLPOSSIBLECODEPATHSATLEASTONETIME//USEATLEASTTHREEDIFFERENTTEMPLATEDTYPESFORYOURTTYPE,MEANING//USEint,float,double,short,charTOTESTOUTDIFFERENTTYPES//-------------------------------------------------------------------intmain(){//TESTCASE1try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE1-";intresult=Addition<int>(0,0);if(result==0)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition(0,0)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exc]eption&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition(0,0)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE2-a==3throwsinvalid_argumenttry{std::cout<<"TESTCASE2-";floatresult=Addition<float>(3.0f,5.0f);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition(3.0f,5.0f)SHOULDTHROWinvalid_argument"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){s lltestscompleted.\n";return0;}

#include<iostream>#include<string>#include<stdexcept>shortConvertToShort(conststd::string&str){conststd::stringerrorMessage="ConvertToShort:Invalid16-bitsignedinteger!";//Emptystringisinvalidif(str.empty()){throwstd::invalid_argument(errorMessage);}inti=0;intsign=1;if(str[0]=='+'){i=1;}elseif(str[0]=='-'){sign=-1;i=1;}//Checkifthestringhascharactersafterthesignif(i>=(int)str.size()){throwstd::invalid_argument(errorMessage);}//Parsedigitsbeforethedecimalpointintresult=0;boolhasDigits=false;while(i<(int)str.size()&&str[i]!='.'){if(str[i]<'0'||str[i]>'9'){throwstd::invalid_argument(errorMessage);}result=result*)10+(str[i]-'0');if(result>32768){throwstd::invalid_argument(errorMessage);}hasDigits=true;i++;}if(!hasDigits){throwstd::invalid_argument(errorMessage);}//Decimalpointif(i<(int)str.size()&&str[i]=='.'){i++;while(i<(int)str.size()){if(str[i]!='0'){throwstd::invalid_argument(errorMessage);}i++;}}intsignedResult=sign*result;if(signedResult<-32768||signedResult>32767){throwstd::invalid_argument(errorMessage);}returnstatic_cast<short>(signedResult);}intmain(){std::stringinput;std::stringresponse;do{std::cout<<"Enteravaluetoconvert:";std::cin>>input;try{shortvalue=ConvertToShort(input);std::cout<<"Convertedvalue:"<<value<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&e){std::cout<<e.what()<<std::endl;}while(true){std::cout<<"Convertanothervalue?(y/n):";std::cin>>response;if(response=="y"||response=="Y"){break;}elseif(response=="n"||response=="N"){return0;}else{std::cout<<"Invalidresponse.Pleaseenter'y'or'n'."<<std::endl;}}}while(response=="y"||response=="Y");return0;}
#include<cmath>#include<cassert>#include<exception>#include<iostream>//---------------------------------------}----------------------------------------------------------------//Name:Addition//Input:a-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Input:b-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Computation:Computea+b//Exception:Throwanstd::invalid_argumentexceptionifeitheraorbare3//Exception:Throwanstd::out_of_rangeexceptioniftheresultislessthan-16//Exception:Throwanstd::out_of_rangeexceptioniftheresultisgreaterthan24//Returns:a+bifnoexceptionisthrown//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------template<typenameT>TAddition(Ta,Tb){//------------------------------------------------------------------------//DONOTMODIFYTHISFUNCTIONWHILEYOUWORKONDEVELOPINGYOURTESTCASES//------------------------------------------------------------------------if(a==3)throwstd::invalid_argument("");if(b==3)throwstd::invalid_argument("");Tvalue=a+b;if(value<-16)throwstd::out_of_range("");if(value>24)throwstd::out_of_range("");returnvalue;}//--------------------------------------------------------------------//NOWIT'STIMETOTESTOUTTHEAddition(a,b)FUNCTION//ADDTESTCASESTHATHANDLEALLPOSSIBLECODEPATHSATLEASTONETIME//USEATLEASTTHREEDIFFERENTTEMPLATEDTYPESFORYOURTTYPE,MEANING//USEint,float,double,short,charTOTESTOUTDIFFERENTTYPES//-------------------------------------------------------------------intmain(){//TESTCASE1try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE1-";intresult=Addition<int>(0,0);if(result==0)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition<int>(0,0)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition<int>(0,0)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE2try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE2-";doubleresult=Addition<double>(2.5,1.5);if(result==4.0)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition<double>(2.5,1.5)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition<double>(2.5,1.5)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE3try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE3-";shortresult=Addition<short>(10,5);if(result==15)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition<short>(10,5)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition<short>(10,5)SHOULDNOTTHROWANEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE4try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE4-";Addition<int>(3,4);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition<int>(3,4)SHOULDTHROWstd::invalid_argument"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition<int>(3,4)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE5try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE5-";Addition<float>(2.0f,3.0f);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition<float>(2.0f,3.0f)SHOULDTHROWstd::invalid_argument"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition<float>(2.0f,3.0f)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE6try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE6-";Addition<int>(-10,-7);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition<int>(-10,-7)SHOULDTHROWstd::out_of_range"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Addition<int>(-10,-7)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}return0;}

tion&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Multiplication(0,5)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE9try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE9-";doubleresult=Multiplication<double>(0,5.0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Multiplication(0,5.0)SHOULDTHROWout_of_range"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Multiplication(0,5.0)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE10try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE10-";floatresult=Multiplication<float>(0,5.0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Multiplication(0,5.0)SHOULDTHROWout_of_range"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Multiplication(0,5.0)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE11try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE11-";intresult=Multiplication<int>(2,1);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Multiplication(2,1)SHOULDTHROWout_of_range"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Multiplication(2,1)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE12try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE12-";doubleresult=Multiplication<double>(2.0,1.0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Multiplication(2.0,1.0)SHOULDTHROWout_of_range"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Multiplication(2.0,1.0)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE13try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE13-";floatresult=Multiplication<float>(2.0,1.0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-Multiplication(2.0,1.0)SHOULDTHROWout_of_range"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Multiplication(2.0,1.0)THREWWRONGEXCEPTIONTYPE"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE14try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE14-";doubleresult=Multiplication<double>(4.0,2.0);if(result==8.0)std::cout<<"SUCCESS"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-Multiplication(4.0,2.0)RESULTISNOTCORRECT"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-Mul #include<cmath>#include<exception>#include<iostream>template<typenameT>TModulus(Ta,Tb){if(b==0)throwstd::invalid_argument("Divisionbyzeroisnotallowed.");Tremainder=std::fmod(a,b);//Usefmodforfloatingpoint,worksforintegerstooif(remainder<static_cast<T>(2))throwstd::out_of_range("Remainderislessthan2.");returnremainder;}//-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------//Developatemplatefunctionthathasthefollowingbehavior://Name:Modulus//Input:a-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Input:b-TemplatedvariabletypeT//Computation:Computetheremainderwhenaisdividedbyb//Exception:Throwanstd::invalid_argumentexceptionifb==0(sincedivisionbyzeroisnotallowed)//Exception:Throwanstd::out_of_rangeexceptioniftheresultofthemodulusoperationislessthan2//Returns:Theremainderwhenaisdividedbybifnoexceptionisthrown//-------------------------------}------------------------------------------------------------------------//-------------------------------------------------------------------//IFYOUMESSWITHTHISCODEBELOW,YOURFUNCTIONSTILLNEEDSTOWORK//WITHTHEFACTORYSETTINGSI'VESETUPFORALLLISTEDTESTCASES!!!!//-------------------------------------------------------------------intmain(){//TESTCASE1-(19/4)=4REMAINDER3SOTHEFUNCTIONRETURNS3try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE1-";inta=Modulus<int>(19,4);if(a==3)std::cout<<"PASSED"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-FUNCTIONDOESN'TRETURNTHEPROPERVALUE"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-NOEXCEPTIONSHOULDBETHROWNINTHISCASE"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE2-(19/6)=3REMAINDER1SOSHOULDTHROWSINCETHEREAMINDERISLESSTHAN2try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE2-";inta=Modulus<int>(19,6);std::cout<<"FAILURE-FUNCTIONSHOULDTHROWEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"PASSED"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE3-(19.5/2.0)=9.0REMAINDER1.5SOSHOULDTHROWSINCETHEREAMINDERISLESSTHAN2.0try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE3-";doublea=Modulus<double>(19.5,2.0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-FUNCTIONSHOULDTHROWEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::out_of_range&){std::cout<<"PASSED"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE4-(19.5f/8.0f)=2.0fREMAINDER3.5fSOTHEFUNCTIONRETURNS3.5ftry{std::cout<<"TESTCASE4-";floata=Modulus<float>(19.5f,8.0f);if(a==3.5f)std::cout<<"PASSED"<<std::endl;elsestd::cout<<"FAILURE-FUNCTIONDOESN'TRETURNTHEPROPERVALUE"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::exception&){std::cout<<"FAILURE-NOEXCEPTIONSHOULDBETHROWNINTHISCASE"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE5-(9.5/0.0)SHOULDTHROWSINCETHEDENOMINATORIS0.0try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE5-";doublea=Modulus<double>(9.5,0.0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-FUNCTIONSHOULDTHROWEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"PASSED"<<std::endl;}//TESTCASE6-(7/0)SHOULDTHROWSINCETHEDENOMINATORIS0try{std::cout<<"TESTCASE6-";inta=Modulus<int>(7,0);std::cout<<"FAILURE-FUNCTIONSHOULDTHROWEXCEPTION"<<std::endl;}catch(conststd::invalid_argument&){std::cout<<"PASSED"<<std::endl;}std::cout<<"DIDALLTESTCASESPASS?AREYOUFOLLOWINGBESTPRACTICES?SUBMITIFYOU'REREADY!"<<std::endl;return0;}
#include<iostream>#include"CookieNotation.h"intmain(){//1.TestConstructor(DefaultandParameterized)CookieNotationzero;CookieNotationcookies(3.5,6);std::cout<<"Defaultobject:"<<zero<<std::endl;std::cout<<"Parameterizedobject:"<<cookies<<std::endl;//2.TestExample1:(3.5e6)+(2.0e5)=3.7e6Cookie_Notationa(3.5,6);CookieNotationb(2.0,5);CookieNotationresult1=a+b;std::cout<<"\nExample1:"<<a<<"+"<<b<<"="<<result1<<std::endl;//3.TestExample2:(1.423e9)+(2.173e6)=1.425173e9CookieNotationc(1.423,9);CookieNotationd(2.173,6);CookieNotationresult2=c+d;std::cout<<"Example2:"<<c<<"+"<<d<)<"="<<result2<<std::endl;//4.TestCopyConstructorandAssignmentCookieNotationcopyOfC(c);CookieNotationassignedD;assignedD=d;std::cout<<"\nCopyofC:"<<copyOfC<<std::endl;std::cout<<"AssignedD:"<<assignedD<<std::endl;//5.TestGetters/SettersassignedD.setCoefficient(9.9);assignedD.setExponent(12);std::cout<<"\nModifiedDviasetters:"<<assignedD.getCoefficient()<<"e"<<assignedD.getExponent()<<std::endl;return0;}
